***изъян.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́н</a> (15527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">زیان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ziyân</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">damage, injury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izʺjátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">withdraw, remove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izʺján</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>defect, fault, stain, loss, flaw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существенный.html>суще́ственный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́н</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V dánnoj sxéme jestʹ suščéstvennyj <b>izʺján</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There is a significant <b>defect</b> in such outline</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:получаться.html>получа́ется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> где́-то вкра́лся <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изъян.html>изъя́н</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A tepérʹ vot polučájetsja, što gdé-to vkrálsja <b>izʺján</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And now it turns out that somewhere a <b>flaw</b> slipped in</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***изъять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a> (6503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">изъяти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izŭjati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьzъjęti</i>, formed as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izʺjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remove, to withdraw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейф.html>се́йфа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izʺjátʹ</b> dokuménty iz séjfa/sɛ́jfa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to remove documents from the safe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:купюра.html>купю́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izʺjátʹ</b> stáryje kupjúry iz oboróta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to withdraw old banknotes from circulation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take away, to confiscate</li></ol>

***изымать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a> (21272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izymátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъять.html>изъя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remove, to withdraw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейф.html>се́йфа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izymátʹ</b> dokuménty iz séjfa/sɛ́jfa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to remove documents from the safe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:купюра.html>купю́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izymátʹ</b> stáryje kupjúry iz oboróta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to withdraw old banknotes from circulation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take away, to confiscate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изыска́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izyskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***икать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:икать.html>ика́ть</a> (18474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьkati</i>, morphologically from onomatopoeic <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-katʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икать.html>ика́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ikátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икнуть.html>икну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hiccup</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икота.html>ико́та</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ikóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-katʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икать.html>и́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pronounce unstressed <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">je</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, to the Standard Russian pronunciation, to rather than as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">je</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>An example is the Standard Russian pronunciation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земля́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zemljá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as <span class="IPA">[zʲɪmˈlʲa]</span>, which could be respelled as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*зимля́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*zimljá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">и́канье</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">íkanʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***икра.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a> (4971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьkrā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ikʷ(e)r-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish egg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Compare Proto-Indo-European to etymology of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">roe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish eggs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ikrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икры́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>и́кры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>и́кр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only singular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> roe, spawn <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of fish</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, also small eggs of frogs or other amphibia
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икру́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">metátʹ <b>ikrú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spawn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only singular</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> caviar <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зернистый.html>зерни́стая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zernístaja <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">soft caviar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ке́товая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kétovaja <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">red caviar<i>, </i>ikra</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">у́стричная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ústričnaja <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">spat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> only singular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paste (dish of mushrooms or vegetables minced into small particles)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">баклажа́нная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">baklažánnaja <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">aubergine paste</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кабачко́вая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kabačkóvaja <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">marrow paste</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грибной.html>грибна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gribnája <b>ikrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mushroom paste</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> calf of the leg, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">musculus gastrocnemius</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> gastrocnemius muscle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>и́крами</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">igrátʹ <b>íkrami</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to repeatedly quickly tense and relax the calves of the legs</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to play with the calves</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drifting ice floe <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially on a river</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ил.html>ил</a> (9068)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">илъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ilŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьlъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ил.html>ил</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">il</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ил.html>и́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ил.html>и́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ил.html>и́лов</a></b>)

***или.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> (54)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + particle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">li</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_4">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">íli</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>or
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xóčešʹ čaj <b>íli</b> kófe?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Do you want tea <b>or</b> coffee?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>or else
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ю</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Idí sjudá, <b>íli</b> tebjá pojmáju!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Come here, <b>or else</b> I'll go get you!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>either
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́т</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>íli</b> tót, <b>íli</b> drugój</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>either</b> the one, <b>or</b> the other</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
